# <a name="routing-in-aspnet-core"></a><span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-103">ASP.NET Core 中的路由</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-103">Routing in ASP.NET Core</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-104">撰写者：[Ryan Nowak](https://github.com/rynowak)、[Steve Smith](https://ardalis.com/) 和 [Rick Anderson](https://twitter.com/RickAndMSFT)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-104">By [Ryan Nowak](https://github.com/rynowak), [Steve Smith](https://ardalis.com/), and [Rick Anderson](https://twitter.com/RickAndMSFT)</span></span>

::: moniker range=">= aspnetcore-3.0"

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-105">路由负责将请求 URI 映射到终结点并向这些终结点调度传入的请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-105">Routing is responsible for mapping request URIs to endpoints and dispatching incoming requests to those endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-106">路由在应用中定义，并在应用启动时进行配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-106">Routes are defined in the app and configured when the app starts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-107">路由可以选择从请求包含的 URL 中提取值，然后这些值便可用于处理请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-107">A route can optionally extract values from the URL contained in the request, and these values can then be used for request processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-108">通过使用应用中的路由信息，路由还能生成映射到终结点的 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-108">Using route information from the app, routing is also able to generate URLs that map to endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-109">许多应用不需要添加模板所提供内容之外的路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-109">Many apps don't need to add routes beyond what the templates provide.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-110">控制器和 Razor 页面的 ASP.NET Core 模板配置路由终结点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-110">The ASP.NET Core templates for controllers and Razor pages configure route endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-111">如果需要添加自定义路由终结点，则可以将自定义终结点与模板生成的路由终结点一起配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-111">If you need to add custom route endpoints, the custom endpoints can be configured alongside template generated route endpoints.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-112">本文档介绍较低级别的 ASP.NET Core 路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-112">This document covers low-level ASP.NET Core routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-113">有关 ASP.NET Core MVC 路由的信息，请参阅 <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-113">For information on ASP.NET Core MVC routing, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-114">有关 Razor Pages 中路由约定的信息，请参阅 <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-114">For information on routing conventions in Razor Pages, see <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-115">[查看或下载示例代码](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples)（[如何下载](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample)）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-115">[View or download sample code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples) ([how to download](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span></span>

## <a name="routing-basics"></a><span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-116">路由基础知识</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-116">Routing basics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-117">大多数应用应选择基本的描述性路由方案，让 URL 有可读性和意义。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-117">Most apps should choose a basic and descriptive routing scheme so that URLs are readable and meaningful.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-118">默认传统路由 `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}`：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-118">The default conventional route `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-119">支持基本的描述性路由方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-119">Supports a basic and descriptive routing scheme.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-120">是基于 UI 的应用的有用起点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-120">Is a useful starting point for UI-based apps.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-121">开发人员通常在专业情况下（例如，博客和电子商务终结点）使用[属性路由](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#attribute-routing)或专用传统路由向应用的高流量区域添加其他简洁路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-121">Developers commonly add additional terse routes to high-traffic areas of an app in specialized situations (for example, blog and ecommerce endpoints) using [attribute routing](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#attribute-routing) or dedicated conventional routes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-122">Web API 应使用属性路由，将应用功能建模为一组资源，其中操作是由 HTTP 谓词表示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-122">Web APIs should use attribute routing to model the app's functionality as a set of resources where operations are represented by HTTP verbs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-123">也就是说，对同一逻辑资源执行的许多操作（例如，GET、POST）都将使用相同 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-123">This means that many operations (for example, GET, POST) on the same logical resource will use the same URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-124">属性路由提供了精心设计 API 的公共终结点布局所需的控制级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-124">Attribute routing provides a level of control that's needed to carefully design an API's public endpoint layout.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-125">Razor Pages 应用使用默认的传统路由从应用的“页面”文件夹中提供命名资源  。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-125">Razor Pages apps use default conventional routing to serve named resources in the *Pages* folder of an app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-126">还可以使用其他约定来自定义 Razor Pages 路由行为。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-126">Additional conventions are available that allow you to customize Razor Pages routing behavior.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-127">有关详细信息，请参阅 <xref:razor-pages/index> 和 <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-127">For more information, see <xref:razor-pages/index> and <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-128">借助 URL 生成支持，无需通过硬编码 URL 将应用关联到一起，即可开发应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-128">URL generation support allows the app to be developed without hard-coding URLs to link the app together.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-129">此支持允许从基本路由配置入手，并在确定应用的资源布局后修改路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-129">This support allows for starting with a basic routing configuration and modifying the routes after the app's resource layout is determined.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-130">路由使用“终结点”(`Endpoint`) 来表示应用中的逻辑终结点  。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-130">Routing uses *endpoints* (`Endpoint`) to represent logical endpoints in an app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-131">终结点定义用于处理请求的委托和任意元数据的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-131">An endpoint defines a delegate to process requests and a collection of arbitrary metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-132">元数据用于实现横切关注点，该实现基于附加到每个终结点的策略和配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-132">The metadata is used to implement cross-cutting concerns based on policies and configuration attached to each endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-133">路由系统具有以下特征：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-133">The routing system has the following characteristics:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-134">路由模板语法用于通过标记化路由参数来定义路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-134">Route template syntax is used to define routes with tokenized route parameters.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-135">可以使用常规样式和属性样式终结点配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-135">Conventional-style and attribute-style endpoint configuration is permitted.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-136"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 用于确定 URL 参数是否包含给定的终结点约束的有效值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-136"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> is used to determine whether a URL parameter contains a valid value for a given endpoint constraint.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-137">应用模型（如 MVC/Razor Pages）注册其所有终结点，这些终结点具有可预测的路由方案实现。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-137">App models, such as MVC/Razor Pages, register all of their endpoints, which have a predictable implementation of routing scenarios.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-138">路由实现会在中间件管道中任何所需位置制定路由决策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-138">The routing implementation makes routing decisions wherever desired in the middleware pipeline.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-139">路由中间件之后出现的中间件可以检查路由中间件针对给定请求 URI 的终结点决策结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-139">Middleware that appears after a Routing Middleware can inspect the result of the Routing Middleware's endpoint decision for a given request URI.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-140">可以在中间件管道中的任何位置枚举应用中的所有终结点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-140">It's possible to enumerate all of the endpoints in the app anywhere in the middleware pipeline.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-141">应用可根据终结点信息使用路由生成 URL（例如，用于重定向或链接），从而避免硬编码 URL，这有助于可维护性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-141">An app can use routing to generate URLs (for example, for redirection or links) based on endpoint information and thus avoid hard-coded URLs, which helps maintainability.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-142">URL 生成是基于支持任意可扩展性的地址：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-142">URL generation is based on addresses, which support arbitrary extensibility:</span></span>

  * <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-143">可以使用[依赖关系注入 (DI)](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection) 在任意位置解析链接生成器 API (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>) 以生成 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-143">The Link Generator API (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>) can be resolved anywhere using [dependency injection (DI)](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection) to generate URLs.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-144">如果无法通过 DI 获得链接生成器 API，则 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> 会提供生成 URL 的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-144">Where the Link Generator API isn't available via DI, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> offers methods to build URLs.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-145">终结点链接仅限于 MVC/Razor Pages 操作和页。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-145">Endpoint linking is limited to MVC/Razor Pages actions and pages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-146">将计划在未来发布的版本中扩展终结点链接的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-146">The expansions of endpoint-linking capabilities is planned for future releases.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-147">路由通过 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RouterMiddleware> 类连接到[中间件](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index)管道。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-147">Routing is connected to the [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) pipeline by the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RouterMiddleware> class.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-148">[ASP.NET Core MVC](xref:mvc/overview) 向中间件管道添加路由，作为其配置的一部分，并处理 MVC 和 Razor Pages 应用中的路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-148">[ASP.NET Core MVC](xref:mvc/overview) adds routing to the middleware pipeline as part of its configuration and handles routing in MVC and Razor Pages apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-149">要了解如何将路由用作独立组件，请参阅[使用路由中间件](#use-routing-middleware)部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-149">To learn how to use routing as a standalone component, see the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section.</span></span>

### <a name="url-matching"></a><span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-150">URL 匹配</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-150">URL matching</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-151">URL 匹配是路由向终结点调度传入请求的过程  。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-151">URL matching is the process by which routing dispatches an incoming request to an *endpoint*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-152">此过程基于 URL 路径中的数据，但可以进行扩展以考虑请求中的任何数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-152">This process is based on data in the URL path but can be extended to consider any data in the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-153">向单独的处理程序调度请求的功能是缩放应用的大小和复杂性的关键。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-153">The ability to dispatch requests to separate handlers is key to scaling the size and complexity of an app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-154">当路由中间件执行时，它会设置终结点 (`Endpoint`) 并将值路由到 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpContext> 上的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-154">When a Routing Middleware executes, it sets an endpoint (`Endpoint`) and route values to a feature on the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpContext>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-155">对于当前请求：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-155">For the current request:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-156">调用 `HttpContext.GetEndpoint` 将获取终结点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-156">Calling `HttpContext.GetEndpoint` gets the endpoint.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-157">`HttpRequest.RouteValues` 将获取路由值的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-157">`HttpRequest.RouteValues` gets the collection of route values.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-158">在路由中间件之后运行的中间件可以看到终结点并采取措施。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-158">Middleware running after the Routing Middleware can see the endpoint and take action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-159">例如，授权中间件可以在终结点的元数据集合中询问授权策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-159">For example, an Authorization Middleware can interrogate the endpoint's metadata collection for an authorization policy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-160">请求处理管道中的所有中间件执行后，将调用所选终结点的委托。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-160">After all of the middleware in the request processing pipeline is executed, the selected endpoint's delegate is invoked.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-161">终结点路由中的路由系统负责所有的调度决策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-161">The routing system in endpoint routing is responsible for all dispatching decisions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-162">由于中间件是基于所选终结点来应用策略，因此任何可能影响调度或安全策略应用的决策都应在路由系统内部制定，这一点很重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-162">Since the middleware applies policies based on the selected endpoint, it's important that any decision that can affect dispatching or the application of security policies is made inside the routing system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-163">执行终结点委托时，将根据迄今执行的请求处理将 [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) 的属性设为适当的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-163">When the endpoint delegate is executed, the properties of [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) are set to appropriate values based on the request processing performed thus far.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-164">[RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values*) 是从路由中生成的路由值的字典  。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-164">[RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values*) is a dictionary of *route values* produced from the route.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-165">这些值通常通过标记 URL 来确定，可用来接受用户输入，或者在应用内作出进一步的调度决策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-165">These values are usually determined by tokenizing the URL and can be used to accept user input or to make further dispatching decisions inside the app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-166">[RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) 是一个与匹配的路由相关的其他数据的属性包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-166">[RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) is a property bag of additional data related to the matched route.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-167">提供 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*> 以支持将状态数据与每个路由相关联，以便应用可根据所匹配的路由作出决策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-167"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*> are provided to support associating state data with each route so that the app can make decisions based on which route matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-168">这些值是开发者定义的，不会影响通过任何方式路由的行为  。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-168">These values are developer-defined and do **not** affect the behavior of routing in any way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-169">此外，存储于 [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) 中的值可以属于任何类型，与 [RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values) 相反，后者必须能够转换为字符串，或从字符串进行转换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-169">Additionally, values stashed in [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) can be of any type, in contrast to [RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values), which must be convertible to and from strings.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-170">[RouteData.Routers](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers) 是参与成功匹配请求的路由的列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-170">[RouteData.Routers](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers) is a list of the routes that took part in successfully matching the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-171">路由可以相互嵌套。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-171">Routes can be nested inside of one another.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-172"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> 属性可以通过导致匹配的逻辑路由树反映该路径。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-172">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> property reflects the path through the logical tree of routes that resulted in a match.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-173">通常情况下，<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> 中的第一项是路由集合，应该用于生成 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-173">Generally, the first item in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> is the route collection and should be used for URL generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-174"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> 中的最后一项是匹配的路由处理程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-174">The last item in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> is the route handler that matched.</span></span>

<a name="lg"></a>

### <a name="url-generation-with-linkgenerator"></a><span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-175">使用 LinkGenerator 的 URL 生成</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-175">URL generation with LinkGenerator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-176">URL 生成是通过其可根据一组路由值创建 URL 路径的过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-176">URL generation is the process by which routing can create a URL path based on a set of route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-177">这需要考虑终结点与访问它们的 URL 之间的逻辑分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-177">This allows for a logical separation between your endpoints and the URLs that access them.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-178">终结点路由包含链接生成器 API (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-178">Endpoint routing includes the Link Generator API (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-179"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> 是可从 DI 检索的单一实例服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-179"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> is a singleton service that can be retrieved from DI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-180">该 API 可在执行请求的上下文之外使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-180">The API can be used outside of the context of an executing request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-181">MVC 的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> 和依赖 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> 的方案（如 [Tag Helpers](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro)、HTML Helpers 和 [Action Results](xref:mvc/controllers/actions)）使用链接生成器提供链接生成功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-181">MVC's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> and scenarios that rely on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper>, such as [Tag Helpers](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro), HTML Helpers, and [Action Results](xref:mvc/controllers/actions), use the link generator to provide link generating capabilities.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-182">链接生成器基于“地址”和“地址方案”概念   。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-182">The link generator is backed by the concept of an *address* and *address schemes*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-183">地址方案是确定哪些终结点用于链接生成的方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-183">An address scheme is a way of determining the endpoints that should be considered for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-184">例如，许多用户熟悉的来自 MVC/Razor Pages 的路由名称和路由值方案都是作为地址方案实现的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-184">For example, the route name and route values scenarios many users are familiar with from MVC/Razor Pages are implemented as an address scheme.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-185">链接生成器可以通过以下扩展方法链接到 MVC/Razor Pages 操作和页面：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-185">The link generator can link to MVC/Razor Pages actions and pages via the following extension methods:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.ControllerLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetPathByAction*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.ControllerLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetUriByAction*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.PageLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetPathByPage*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.PageLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetUriByPage*>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-186">这些方法的重载接受包含 `HttpContext` 的参数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-186">An overload of these methods accepts arguments that include the `HttpContext`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-187">这些方法在功能上等同于 `Url.Action` 和 `Url.Page`，但提供了更大的灵活性和更多的选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-187">These methods are functionally equivalent to `Url.Action` and `Url.Page` but offer additional flexibility and options.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-188">`GetPath*` 方法与 `Url.Action` 和 `Url.Page` 最相似，因为它们生成包含绝对路径的 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-188">The `GetPath*` methods are most similar to `Url.Action` and `Url.Page` in that they generate a URI containing an absolute path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-189">`GetUri*` 方法始终生成包含方案和主机的绝对 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-189">The `GetUri*` methods always generate an absolute URI containing a scheme and host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-190">接受 `HttpContext` 的方法在执行请求的上下文中生成 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-190">The methods that accept an `HttpContext` generate a URI in the context of the executing request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-191">除非重写，否则将使用来自执行请求的环境路由值、URL 基本路径、方案和主机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-191">The ambient route values, URL base path, scheme, and host from the executing request are used unless overridden.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-192">使用地址调用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-192"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> is called with an address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-193">生成 URI 的过程分两步进行：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-193">Generating a URI occurs in two steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-194">将地址绑定到与地址匹配的终结点列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-194">An address is bound to a list of endpoints that match the address.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-195">计算每个终结点的 `RoutePattern`，直到找到与提供的值匹配的路由模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-195">Each endpoint's `RoutePattern` is evaluated until a route pattern that matches the supplied values is found.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-196">输出结果会与提供给链接生成器的其他 URI 部分进行组合并返回。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-196">The resulting output is combined with the other URI parts supplied to the link generator and returned.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-197">对任何类型的地址，<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> 提供的方法均支持标准链接生成功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-197">The methods provided by <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> support standard link generation capabilities for any type of address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-198">使用链接生成器的最简便方法是通过扩展方法对特定地址类型执行操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-198">The most convenient way to use the link generator is through extension methods that perform operations for a specific address type.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-199">扩展方法</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-199">Extension Method</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-200">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-200">Description</span></span> |
| ---------------- | ----------- |
| <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetPathByAddress*> | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-201">根据提供的值生成具有绝对路径的 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-201">Generates a URI with an absolute path based on the provided values.</span></span> |
| <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetUriByAddress*> | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-202">根据提供的值生成绝对 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-202">Generates an absolute URI based on the provided values.</span></span>             |

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-203">请注意有关调用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> 方法的下列含义：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-203">Pay attention to the following implications of calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> methods:</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-204">对于不验证传入请求的 `Host` 标头的应用配置，请谨慎使用 `GetUri*` 扩展方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-204">Use `GetUri*` extension methods with caution in an app configuration that doesn't validate the `Host` header of incoming requests.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-205">如果未验证传入请求的 `Host`标头，则可能以视图/页面中 URI 的形式将不受信任的请求输入发送回客户端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-205">If the `Host` header of incoming requests isn't validated, untrusted request input can be sent back to the client in URIs in a view/page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-206">建议所有生产应用都将其服务器配置为针对已知有效值验证 `Host` 标头。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-206">We recommend that all production apps configure their server to validate the `Host` header against known valid values.</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-207">在中间件中将 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> 与 `Map` 或 `MapWhen` 结合使用时，请小心谨慎。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-207">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> with caution in middleware in combination with `Map` or `MapWhen`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-208">`Map*` 会更改执行请求的基路径，这会影响链接生成的输出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-208">`Map*` changes the base path of the executing request, which affects the output of link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-209">所有 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API 都允许指定基路径。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-209">All of the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> APIs allow specifying a base path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-210">始终指定一个空的基路径来撤消 `Map*` 对链接生成的影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-210">Always specify an empty base path to undo `Map*`'s affect on link generation.</span></span>

## <a name="endpoint-routing"></a><span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-211">终结点路由</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-211">Endpoint routing</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-212">路由终结点具有模板、元数据以及为终结点响应提供服务的请求委托。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-212">A route endpoint has a template, metadata, and a request delegate that serves the endpoint's response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-213">元数据用于实现横切关注点，该实现基于附加到每个终结点的策略和配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-213">The metadata is used to implement cross-cutting concerns based on policies and configuration attached to each endpoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-214">例如，授权中间件可以在终结点的元数据集合中询问[授权策略](xref:security/authorization/policies#applying-policies-to-mvc-controllers)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-214">For example, an authorization middleware can interrogate the endpoint's metadata collection for an [authorization policy](xref:security/authorization/policies#applying-policies-to-mvc-controllers).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-215">终结点路由使用两个扩展方法与中间件集成：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-215">Endpoint routing integrates with middleware using two extension methods:</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-216">[UseRouting](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*) 向中间件管道添加路由匹配。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-216">[UseRouting](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*) adds route matching to the middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-217">它必须在任何路由感知中间件（如授权、终结点执行等）之前。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-217">It must come before any route-aware middleware such as authorization, endpoint execution, etc.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-218">[UseEndpoints](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*) 向中间件管道添加终结点执行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-218">[UseEndpoints](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*) adds endpoint execution to the middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-219">它运行为终结点响应提供服务的请求委托。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-219">It runs the request delegate that serves the endpoint's response.</span></span>
  <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-220">此外，`UseEndpoints` 还是配置可由应用匹配和执行的路由终结点的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-220">`UseEndpoints` is also where route endpoints are configured that can be matched and executed by the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-221">例如：<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RazorPagesEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRazorPages*>、<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllers*>、<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> 和 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-221">For example, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RazorPagesEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRazorPages*>, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllers*>, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-222">应用使用 ASP.NET Core 的 Helper 方法来配置其路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-222">Apps use ASP.NET Core's helper methods to configure their routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-223">ASP.NET Core 框架提供了 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RazorPagesEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRazorPages*>、<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllers*> 和 `MapHub<THub>` 等 Helper 方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-223">ASP.NET Core frameworks provide helper methods like <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RazorPagesEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRazorPages*>,, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllers*> and `MapHub<THub>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-224">还提供了用于配置自己的自定义路由终结点的 Helper 方法：<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>、<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*> 和 [MapVerb](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-224">There are also helper methods for configuring your own custom route endpoints: <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>, and [MapVerb](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions).</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-225">终结点路由还支持在应用程序启动后更改终结点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-225">Endpoint routing also supports endpoints changing after an application has started up.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-226">若要在应用或 ASP.NET Core 框架中支持这一点，必须创建并注册自定义 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointDataSource>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-226">To support this in your app or ASP.NET Core framework, a custom <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointDataSource> must be created and registered.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-227">这是一项高级功能，通常不需要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-227">This is an advanced feature, and usually not needed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-228">终结点通常在启动时配置，并且在应用的生存期内是静态的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-228">Endpoints are typically configured at startup and are static for the lifetime of the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-229">在启动时从文件或数据库加载路由配置不是动态的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-229">Loading route configuration from a file or database at startup is not dynamic.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-230">以下代码演示终结点路由的基本示例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-230">The following code shows a basic example of endpoint routing:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/Startup.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-231">有关终结点路由的详细信息，请参阅本文档中的 [URL 匹配](#url-matching)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-231">See [URL matching](#url-matching) in this document for more information on endpoint routing.</span></span>

## <a name="endpoint-routing-differences-from-earlier-versions-of-routing"></a><span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-232">终结点路由与早期版本路由的差异</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-232">Endpoint routing differences from earlier versions of routing</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-233">比 ASP.NET Core 2.2 更早的版本中的终结点路由与版本路由之间存在一些差异：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-233">A few differences exist between endpoint routing and versions of routing earlier than in ASP.NET Core 2.2:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-234">终结点路由系统不支持基于 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> 的可扩展性，包括从 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 继承。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-234">The endpoint routing system doesn't support <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based extensibility, including inheriting from <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-235">终结点路由不支持 [WebApiCompatShim](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.WebApiCompatShim)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-235">Endpoint routing doesn't support [WebApiCompatShim](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.WebApiCompatShim).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-236">使用 2.1 [兼容性版本](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) (`.SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_1)`) 以继续使用兼容性填充码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-236">Use the 2.1 [compatibility version](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) (`.SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_1)`) to continue using the compatibility shim.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-237">在使用传统路由时，终结点路由对生成的 URI 的大小写具有不同的行为。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-237">Endpoint Routing has different behavior for the casing of generated URIs when using conventional routes.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-238">请考虑以下默认路由模板：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-238">Consider the following default route template:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  app.UseMvc(routes =>
  {
      routes.MapRoute("default", "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
  });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-239">假设使用以下路由生成某个操作的链接：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-239">Suppose you generate a link to an action using the following route:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  var link = Url.Action("ReadPost", "blog", new { id = 17, });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-240">如果使用基于 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> 的路由，此代码生成 URI `/blog/ReadPost/17`，该 URI 遵循所提供路由值的大小写。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-240">With <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based routing, this code generates a URI of `/blog/ReadPost/17`, which respects the casing of the provided route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-241">ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更高版本中的终结点路由生成 `/Blog/ReadPost/17`（“Blog”大写）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-241">Endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later produces `/Blog/ReadPost/17` ("Blog" is capitalized).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-242">终结点路由提供 `IOutboundParameterTransformer` 接口，可用于在全局范围自定义此行为或应用不同的约定来映射 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-242">Endpoint routing provides the `IOutboundParameterTransformer` interface that can be used to customize this behavior globally or to apply different conventions for mapping URLs.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-243">有关详细信息，请参阅[参数转换器参考](#parameter-transformer-reference)部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-243">For more information, see the [Parameter transformer reference](#parameter-transformer-reference) section.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-244">在试图链接到不存在的控制器/操作或页面时，MVC/Razor Pages 通过传统路由执行的链接生成，其操作具有不同的行为。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-244">Link Generation used by MVC/Razor Pages with conventional routes behaves differently when attempting to link to an controller/action or page that doesn't exist.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-245">请考虑以下默认路由模板：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-245">Consider the following default route template:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  app.UseMvc(routes =>
  {
      routes.MapRoute("default", "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
  });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-246">假设使用以下路由通过默认模板生成某个操作的链接：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-246">Suppose you generate a link to an action using the default template with the following:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  var link = Url.Action("ReadPost", "Blog", new { id = 17, });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-247">如果使用基于 `IRouter` 的路由，即使 `BlogController` 不存在或没有 `ReadPost` 操作方法，结果也始终为 `/Blog/ReadPost/17`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-247">With `IRouter`-based routing, the result is always `/Blog/ReadPost/17`, even if the `BlogController` doesn't exist or doesn't have a `ReadPost` action method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-248">正如所料，如果操作方法存在，ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更高版本中的终结点路由会生成 `/Blog/ReadPost/17`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-248">As expected, endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later produces `/Blog/ReadPost/17` if the action method exists.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-249">但是，如果操作不存在，终结点路由会生成空字符串。 </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-249">*However, endpoint routing produces an empty string if the action doesn't exist.*</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-250">从概念上讲，如果操作不存在，终结点路由不会假定终结点存在。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-250">Conceptually, endpoint routing doesn't assume that the endpoint exists if the action doesn't exist.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-251">与终结点路由一起使用时，链接生成环境值失效算法的行为会有所不同  。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-251">The link generation *ambient value invalidation algorithm* behaves differently when used with endpoint routing.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-252">*环境值失效*是一种算法，用于决定当前正在执行的请求（环境值）中的哪些路由值可用于链接生成操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-252">*Ambient value invalidation* is the algorithm that decides which route values from the currently executing request (the ambient values) can be used in link generation operations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-253">链接到不同操作时，传统路由会使额外的路由值失效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-253">Conventional routing always invalidated extra route values when linking to a different action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-254">ASP.NET Core 2.2 之前的版本中，属性路由不具有此行为。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-254">Attribute routing didn't have this behavior prior to the release of ASP.NET Core 2.2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-255">在 ASP.NET Core 的早期版本中，如果有另一个操作使用同一路由参数名称，则该操作的链接会导致发生链接生成错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-255">In earlier versions of ASP.NET Core, links to another action that use the same route parameter names resulted in link generation errors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-256">在 ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更高版本中，链接到另一个操作时，这两种路由形式都会使值失效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-256">In ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later, both forms of routing invalidate values when linking to another action.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-257">请考虑 ASP.NET Core2.1 或更高版本中的以下示例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-257">Consider the following example in ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-258">链接到另一个操作（或另一页面）时，路由值可能会按非预期的方式被重用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-258">When linking to another action (or another page), route values can be reused in undesirable ways.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-259">在 /Pages/Store/Product.cshtml 中  ：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-259">In */Pages/Store/Product.cshtml*:</span></span>

  ```cshtml
  @page "{id}"
  @Url.Page("/Login")
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-260">在 /Pages/Login.cshtml 中  ：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-260">In */Pages/Login.cshtml*:</span></span>

  ```cshtml
  @page "{id?}"
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-261">如果 ASP.NET Core 2.1 或更早版本中的 URI 为 `/Store/Product/18`，则由 `@Url.Page("/Login")` 在 Store/Info 页面上生成的链接为 `/Login/18`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-261">If the URI is `/Store/Product/18` in ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier, the link generated on the Store/Info page by `@Url.Page("/Login")` is `/Login/18`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-262">即使链接目标完全是应用的其他部分，仍会重用 `id` 值 18。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-262">The `id` value of 18 is reused, even though the link destination is different part of the app entirely.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-263">`/Login` 页面上下文中的 `id` 路由值可能是用户 ID 值，而非存储产品 ID 值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-263">The `id` route value in the context of the `/Login` page is probably a user ID value, not a store product ID value.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-264">在 ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更高版本的终结点路由中，结果为 `/Login`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-264">In endpoint routing with ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later, the result is `/Login`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-265">当链接的目标是另一个操作或页面时，不会重复使用环境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-265">Ambient values aren't reused when the linked destination is a different action or page.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-266">往返路由参数语法：使用双星号 (`**`) catch-all 参数语法时，不对正斜杠进行编码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-266">Round-tripping route parameter syntax: Forward slashes aren't encoded when using a double-asterisk (`**`) catch-all parameter syntax.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-267">在链接生成期间，路由系统对双星号 (`**`) catch-all 参数（例如，`{**myparametername}`）中捕获的除正斜杠外的值进行编码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-267">During link generation, the routing system encodes the value captured in a double-asterisk (`**`) catch-all parameter (for example, `{**myparametername}`) except the forward slashes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-268">在 ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更高版本中，基于 `IRouter` 的路由支持双星号 catch-all 参数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-268">The double-asterisk catch-all is supported with `IRouter`-based routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-269">ASP.NET Core (`{*myparametername}`) 早期版本中的单星号 catch-all 参数语法仍然受支持，并对正斜杠进行编码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-269">The single asterisk catch-all parameter syntax in prior versions of ASP.NET Core (`{*myparametername}`) remains supported, and forward slashes are encoded.</span></span>

  | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-270">路由</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-270">Route</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-271">链接生成方式为</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-271">Link generated with</span></span><br>`Url.Action(new { category = "admin/products" })`&hellip; |
  | ------------------ | --------------------------------------------------------------------- |
  | `/search/{*page}`  | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-272">`/search/admin%2Fproducts`（对正斜杠进行编码）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-272">`/search/admin%2Fproducts` (the forward slash is encoded)</span></span>             |
  | `/search/{**page}` | `/search/admin/products`                                              |

### <a name="middleware-example"></a><span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-273">中间件示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-273">Middleware example</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-274">在以下示例中，中间件使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API 创建列出存储产品的操作方法的链接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-274">In the following example, a middleware uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API to create link to an action method that lists store products.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-275">应用中的任何类都可通过将链接生成器注入类并调用 `GenerateLink` 来使用链接生成器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-275">Using the link generator by injecting it into a class and calling `GenerateLink` is available to any class in an app.</span></span>

```csharp
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing;

public class ProductsLinkMiddleware
{
    private readonly LinkGenerator _linkGenerator;

    public ProductsLinkMiddleware(RequestDelegate next, LinkGenerator linkGenerator)
    {
        _linkGenerator = linkGenerator;
    }

    public async Task InvokeAsync(HttpContext httpContext)
    {
        var url = _linkGenerator.GetPathByAction("ListProducts", "Store");

        httpContext.Response.ContentType = "text/plain";

        await httpContext.Response.WriteAsync($"Go to {url} to see our products.");
    }
}
```

### <a name="create-routes"></a><span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-276">创建路由</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-276">Create routes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-277">大多数应用通过调用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 或 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> 上定义的一种类似的扩展方法来创建路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-277">Most apps create routes by calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> or one of the similar extension methods defined on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-278">任何 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> 扩展方法都会创建 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 的实例并将其添加到路由集合中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-278">Any of the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> extension methods create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> and add it to the route collection.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-279"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 不接受路由处理程序参数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-279"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> doesn't accept a route handler parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-280"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 仅添加由 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*> 处理的路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-280"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> only adds routes that are handled by the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-281">要了解 MVC 中的路由的详细信息，请参阅 <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-281">To learn more about routing in MVC, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-282">以下代码示例是典型 ASP.NET Core MVC 路由定义使用的一个 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 调用示例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-282">The following code example is an example of a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> call used by a typical ASP.NET Core MVC route definition:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-283">此模板与 URL 路径相匹配，并且提取路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-283">This template matches a URL path and extracts the route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-284">例如，路径 `/Products/Details/17` 生成以下路由值：`{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 17 }`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-284">For example, the path `/Products/Details/17` generates the following route values: `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 17 }`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-285">路由值是通过将 URL 路径拆分成段，并且将每段与路由模板中的路由参数名称相匹配来确定的  。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-285">Route values are determined by splitting the URL path into segments and matching each segment with the *route parameter* name in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-286">路由参数已命名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-286">Route parameters are named.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-287">参数通过将参数名称括在大括号 `{ ... }` 中来定义。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-287">The parameters defined by enclosing the parameter name in braces `{ ... }`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-288">上述模板还可匹配 URL 路径 `/`，并且生成值 `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-288">The preceding template could also match the URL path `/` and produce the values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-289">这是因为 `{controller}` 和 `{action}` 路由参数具有默认值，且 `id` 路由参数是可选的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-289">This occurs because the `{controller}` and `{action}` route parameters have default values and the `id` route parameter is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-290">路由参数名称为参数定义默认值后，等号 (`=`) 后将有一个值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-290">An equals sign (`=`) followed by a value after the route parameter name defines a default value for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-291">路由参数名称后面的问号 (`?`) 定义了可选参数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-291">A question mark (`?`) after the route parameter name defines an optional parameter.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-292">路由匹配时，具有默认值的路由参数始终会生成路由值  。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-292">Route parameters with a default value *always* produce a route value when the route matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-293">如果没有相应的 URL 路径段，则可选参数不会生成路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-293">Optional parameters don't produce a route value if there was no corresponding URL path segment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-294">有关路由模板方案和语法的详细说明，请参阅[路由模板参考](#route-template-reference)部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-294">See the [Route template reference](#route-template-reference) section for a thorough description of route template scenarios and syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-295">在以下示例中，路由参数定义 `{id:int}` 为 `id` 路由参数定义[路由约束](#route-constraint-reference)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-295">In the following example, the route parameter definition `{id:int}` defines a [route constraint](#route-constraint-reference) for the `id` route parameter:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id:int}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-296">此模板与类似于 `/Products/Details/17` 而不是 `/Products/Details/Apples` 的 URL 路径相匹配。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-296">This template matches a URL path like `/Products/Details/17` but not `/Products/Details/Apples`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-297">路由约束实现 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 并检查路由值，以验证它们。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-297">Route constraints implement <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> and inspect route values to verify them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-298">在此示例中，路由值 `id` 必须可转换为整数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-298">In this example, the route value `id` must be convertible to an integer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-299">有关框架提供的路由约束的说明，请参阅[路由约束参考](#route-constraint-reference)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-299">See [route-constraint-reference](#route-constraint-reference) for an explanation of route constraints provided by the framework.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-300">其他 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 重载接受 `constraints`、`dataTokens` 和 `defaults` 的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-300">Additional overloads of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> accept values for `constraints`, `dataTokens`, and `defaults`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-301">这些参数的典型用法是传递匿名类型化对象，其中匿名类型的属性名匹配路由参数名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-301">The typical usage of these parameters is to pass an anonymously typed object, where the property names of the anonymous type match route parameter names.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-302">以下 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 示例可创建等效路由：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-302">The following <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> examples create equivalent routes:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller}/{action}/{id?}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Home", action = "Index" });

routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-303">定义约束和默认值的内联语法对于简单路由很方便。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-303">The inline syntax for defining constraints and defaults can be convenient for simple routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-304">但是，存在内联语法不支持的方案，例如数据令牌。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-304">However, there are scenarios, such as data tokens, that aren't supported by inline syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-305">以下示例演示了一些其他方案：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-305">The following example demonstrates a few additional scenarios:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "blog",
    template: "Blog/{**article}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadArticle" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-306">上述模板与 `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` 等的 URL 路径相匹配，并提取值 `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-306">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` and extracts the values `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-307">`controller` 和 `action` 的默认路由值由路由生成，即便模板中没有对应的路由参数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-307">The default route values for `controller` and `action` are produced by the route even though there are no corresponding route parameters in the template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-308">可在路由模板中指定默认值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-308">Default values can be specified in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-309">根据路由参数名称前的双星号 (`**`) 外观，`article` 路由参数被定义为 catch-all  。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-309">The `article` route parameter is defined as a *catch-all* by the appearance of an double asterisk (`**`) before the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-310">全方位路由参数可捕获 URL 路径的其余部分，也能匹配空白字符串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-310">Catch-all route parameters capture the remainder of the URL path and can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-311">以下示例添加了路由约束和数据令牌：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-311">The following example adds route constraints and data tokens:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "us_english_products",
    template: "en-US/Products/{id}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Products", action = "Details" },
    constraints: new { id = new IntRouteConstraint() },
    dataTokens: new { locale = "en-US" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-312">上述模板与 `/en-US/Products/5` 等 URL 路径相匹配，并且提取值 `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` 和数据令牌 `{ locale = en-US }`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-312">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/en-US/Products/5` and extracts the values `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` and the data tokens `{ locale = en-US }`.</span></span>

![本地 Windows 令牌](routing/_static/tokens.png)

### <a name="route-class-url-generation"></a><span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-314">路由类 URL 生成</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-314">Route class URL generation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-315"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 类还可通过将一组路由值与其路由模板组合来生成 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-315">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class can also perform URL generation by combining a set of route values with its route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-316">从逻辑上来说，这是匹配 URL 路径的反向过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-316">This is logically the reverse process of matching the URL path.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-317">为更好了解 URL 生成，请想象你要生成的 URL，然后考虑路由模板将如何匹配该 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-317">To better understand URL generation, imagine what URL you want to generate and then think about how a route template would match that URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-318">将生成什么值？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-318">What values would be produced?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-319">这大致相当于 URL 在 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 类中的生成方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-319">This is the rough equivalent of how URL generation works in the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-320">以下示例使用常规 ASP.NET Core MVC 默认路由：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-320">The following example uses a general ASP.NET Core MVC default route:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-321">使用路由值 `{ controller = Products, action = List }`，将生成 URL `/Products/List`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-321">With the route values `{ controller = Products, action = List }`, the URL `/Products/List` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-322">路由值将替换为相应的路由参数，以形成 URL 路径。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-322">The route values are substituted for the corresponding route parameters to form the URL path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-323">由于 `id` 是可选路由参数，因此成功生成的 URL 不具有 `id` 的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-323">Since `id` is an optional route parameter, the URL is successfully generated without a value for `id`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-324">使用路由值 `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`，将生成 URL `/`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-324">With the route values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`, the URL `/` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-325">提供的路由值与默认值匹配，并且会安全地省略与默认值对应的段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-325">The provided route values match the default values, and the segments corresponding to the default values are safely omitted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-326">已生成的两个 URL 将往返以下路由定义 (`/Home/Index` 和 `/`)，并生成用于生成该 URL 的相同路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-326">Both URLs generated round-trip with the following route definition (`/Home/Index` and `/`) produce the same route values that were used to generate the URL.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-327">使用 ASP.NET Core MVC 应用应该使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> 生成 URL，而不是直接调用到路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-327">An app using ASP.NET Core MVC should use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> to generate URLs instead of calling into routing directly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-328">有关 URL 生成的详细信息，请参阅 [Url 生成参考](#url-generation-reference)部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-328">For more information on URL generation, see the [Url generation reference](#url-generation-reference) section.</span></span>

## <a name="use-routing-middleware"></a><span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-329">使用路由中间件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-329">Use Routing Middleware</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-330">引用应用项目文件中的 [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App 元包](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-330">Reference the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App metapackage](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) in the app's project file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-331">将路由添加到 `Startup.ConfigureServices` 中的服务容器：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-331">Add routing to the service container in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_ConfigureServices&highlight=3)]

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-332">必须在 `Startup.Configure` 方法中配置路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-332">Routes must be configured in the `Startup.Configure` method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-333">该示例应用使用以下 API：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-333">The sample app uses the following APIs:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>
* <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-334"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> &ndash; 仅匹配 HTTP GET 请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-334"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> &ndash; Matches only HTTP GET requests.</span></span>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_RouteHandler)]

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-335">下表显示了具有给定 URI 的响应。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-335">The following table shows the responses with the given URIs.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-336">URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-336">URI</span></span>                    | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-337">响应</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-337">Response</span></span>                                          |
| ---------------------- | ------------------------------------------------- |
| `/package/create/3`    | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-338">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-338">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-339">Route values: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-339">Route values: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3`    | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-340">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-340">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-341">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-341">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3/`   | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-342">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-342">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-343">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-343">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/`      | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-344">请求失败，不匹配。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-344">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |
| `GET /hello/Joe`       | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-345">Hi, Joe!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-345">Hi, Joe!</span></span>                                          |
| `POST /hello/Joe`      | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-346">请求失败，仅匹配 HTTP GET。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-346">The request falls through, matches HTTP GET only.</span></span> |
| `GET /hello/Joe/Smith` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-347">请求失败，不匹配。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-347">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-348">框架可提供一组用于创建路由 (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>) 的扩展方法：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-348">The framework provides a set of extension methods for creating routes (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareVerb*>
