| <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1233">约束</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1233">constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1234">示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1234">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1235">匹配项示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1235">Example Matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1236">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1236">Notes</span></span> |
| ---------- | ------- | --------------- | ----- |
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1237">`123456789`，`-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1237">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1238">匹配任何整数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1238">Matches any integer</span></span> |
| `bool` | `{active:bool}` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1239">`true`，`FALSE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1239">`true`, `FALSE`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1240">匹配 `true`或 `false`（区分大小写）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1240">Matches `true` or `false` (case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `datetime` | `{dob:datetime}` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1241">`2016-12-31`，`2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1241">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1242">匹配有效的 `DateTime` 值（位于固定区域性中 - 查看警告）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1242">Matches a valid `DateTime` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `decimal` | `{price:decimal}` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1243">`49.99`，`-1,000.01`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1243">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1244">匹配有效的 `decimal` 值（位于固定区域性中 - 查看警告）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1244">Matches a valid `decimal` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `double` | `{weight:double}` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1245">`1.234`，`-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1245">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1246">匹配有效的 `double` 值（位于固定区域性中 - 查看警告）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1246">Matches a valid `double` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `float` | `{weight:float}` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1247">`1.234`，`-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1247">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1248">匹配有效的 `float` 值（位于固定区域性中 - 查看警告）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1248">Matches a valid `float` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `guid` | `{id:guid}` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1249">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`，`{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1249">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1250">匹配有效的 `Guid` 值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1250">Matches a valid `Guid` value</span></span> |
| `long` | `{ticks:long}` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1251">`123456789`，`-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1251">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1252">匹配有效的 `long` 值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1252">Matches a valid `long` value</span></span> |
| `minlength(value)` | `{username:minlength(4)}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1253">字符串必须至少为 4 个字符</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1253">String must be at least 4 characters</span></span> |
| `maxlength(value)` | `{filename:maxlength(8)}` | `Richard` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1254">字符串不得超过 8 个字符</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1254">String must be no more than 8 characters</span></span> |
| `length(length)` | `{filename:length(12)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1255">字符串必须正好为 12 个字符</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1255">String must be exactly 12 characters long</span></span> |
| `length(min,max)` | `{filename:length(8,16)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1256">字符串必须至少为 8 个字符，且不得超过 16 个字符</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1256">String must be at least 8 and no more than 16 characters long</span></span> |
| `min(value)` | `{age:min(18)}` | `19` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1257">整数值必须至少为 18</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1257">Integer value must be at least 18</span></span> |
| `max(value)` | `{age:max(120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1258">整数值不得超过 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1258">Integer value must be no more than 120</span></span> |
| `range(min,max)` | `{age:range(18,120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1259">整数值必须至少为 18，且不得超过 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1259">Integer value must be at least 18 but no more than 120</span></span> |
| `alpha` | `{name:alpha}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1260">字符串必须由一个或多个字母字符（`a`-`z`，区分大小写）组成</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1260">String must consist of one or more alphabetical characters (`a`-`z`, case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `regex(expression)` | `{ssn:regex(^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$)}` | `123-45-6789` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1261">字符串必须匹配正则表达式（参见有关定义正则表达式的提示）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1261">String must match the regular expression (see tips about defining a regular expression)</span></span> |
| `required` | `{name:required}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1262">用于强制在 URL 生成过程中存在非参数值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1262">Used to enforce that a non-parameter value is present during URL generation</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1263">可向单个参数应用多个由冒号分隔的约束。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1263">Multiple, colon-delimited constraints can be applied to a single parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1264">例如，以下约束将参数限制为大于或等于 1 的整数值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1264">For example, the following constraint restricts a parameter to an integer value of 1 or greater:</span></span>

```csharp
[Route("users/{id:int:min(1)}")]
public User GetUserById(int id) { }
```

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1265">验证 URL 的路由约束并将转换为始终使用固定区域性的 CLR 类型（例如 `int` 或 `DateTime`）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1265">Route constraints that verify the URL and are converted to a CLR type (such as `int` or `DateTime`) always use the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1266">这些约束假定 URL 不可本地化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1266">These constraints assume that the URL is non-localizable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1267">框架提供的路由约束不会修改存储于路由值中的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1267">The framework-provided route constraints don't modify the values stored in route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1268">从 URL 中分析的所有路由值都将存储为字符串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1268">All route values parsed from the URL are stored as strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1269">例如，`float` 约束会尝试将路由值转换为浮点数，但转换后的值仅用来验证其是否可转换为浮点数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1269">For example, the `float` constraint attempts to convert the route value to a float, but the converted value is used only to verify it can be converted to a float.</span></span>

## <a name="regular-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1270">正则表达式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1270">Regular expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1271">ASP.NET Core 框架将向正则表达式构造函数添加 `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1271">The ASP.NET Core framework adds `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` to the regular expression constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1272">有关这些成员的说明，请参阅 <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1272">See <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> for a description of these members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1273">正则表达式与路由和 C# 计算机语言使用的分隔符和令牌相似。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1273">Regular expressions use delimiters and tokens similar to those used by Routing and the C# language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1274">必须对正则表达式令牌进行转义。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1274">Regular expression tokens must be escaped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1275">要在路由中使用正则表达式 `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$`，表达式必须在字符串中提供 `\`（单反斜杠）字符，正如 C# 源文件中的 `\\`（双反斜杠）字符一样，以便对 `\` 字符串转义字符进行转义（除非使用[字符串文本](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1275">To use the regular expression `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in routing, the expression must have the `\` (single backslash) characters provided in the string as `\\` (double backslash) characters in the C# source file in order to escape the `\` string escape character (unless using [verbatim string literals](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1276">要对路由参数分隔符进行转义（`{`、`}`、`[`、`]`），请将表达式（`{{`、`}`、`[[`、`]]`）中的字符数加倍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1276">To escape routing parameter delimiter characters (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), double the characters in the expression (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1277">下表展示了正则表达式和转义版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1277">The following table shows a regular expression and the escaped version.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1278">正则表达式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1278">Regular Expression</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1279">转义后的正则表达式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1279">Escaped Regular Expression</span></span>     |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1280">路由中使用的正则表达式通常以脱字号 (`^`) 开头，并匹配字符串的起始位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1280">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the caret (`^`) character and match starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1281">表达式通常以美元符号 (`$`) 字符结尾，并匹配字符串的结尾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1281">The expressions often end with the dollar sign (`$`) character and match end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1282">`^` 和 `$` 字符可确保正则表达式匹配整个路由参数值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1282">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression match the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1283">如果没有 `^` 和 `$` 字符，正则表达式将匹配字符串内的所有子字符串，而这通常是不需要的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1283">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression match any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1284">下表提供了示例并说明了它们匹配或匹配失败的原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1284">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1285">表达式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1285">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1286">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1286">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1287">匹配</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1287">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1288">注释</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1288">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1289">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1289">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1290">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1290">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1291">子字符串匹配</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1291">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1292">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1292">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1293">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1293">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1294">子字符串匹配</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1294">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1295">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1295">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1296">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1296">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1297">匹配表达式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1297">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1298">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1298">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1299">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1299">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1300">不区分大小写</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1300">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1301">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1301">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1302">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1302">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1303">参阅上述 `^` 和 `$`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1303">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1304">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1304">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1305">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1305">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1306">参阅上述 `^` 和 `$`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1306">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1307">有关正则表达式语法的详细信息，请参阅 [.NET Framework 正则表达式](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1307">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1308">若要将参数限制为一组已知的可能值，可使用正则表达式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1308">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1309">例如，`{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` 仅将 `action` 路由值匹配到 `list`、`get` 或 `create`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1309">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1310">如果传递到约束字典中，字符串 `^(list|get|create)$` 将等效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1310">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1311">已传递到约束字典（不与模板内联）且不匹配任何已知约束的约束还将被视为正则表达式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1311">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary (not inline within a template) that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

## <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1312">自定义路由约束</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1312">Custom Route Constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1313">除了内置路由约束以外，还可以通过实现 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 接口来创建自定义路由约束。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1313">In addition to the built-in route constraints, custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1314"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 接口包含一个方法 `Match`，当满足约束时，它返回 `true`，否则返回 `false`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1314">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface contains a single method, `Match`, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1315">若要使用自定义 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>，必须在应用的服务容器中使用应用的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 注册路由约束类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1315">To use a custom <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the app's service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1316"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 是将路由约束键映射到验证这些约束的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 实现的目录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1316">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1317">应用的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 可作为 [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) 调用的一部分在 `Startup.ConfigureServices` 中进行更新，也可以通过使用 `services.Configure<RouteOptions>` 直接配置 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> 进行更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1317">An app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1318">例如：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1318">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    options.ConstraintMap.Add("customName", typeof(MyCustomConstraint));
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1319">然后，可以使用在注册约束类型时指定的名称，以常规方式将约束应用于路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1319">The constraint can then be applied to routes in the usual manner, using the name specified when registering the constraint type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1320">例如：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1320">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
[HttpGet("{id:customName}")]
public ActionResult<string> Get(string id)
```

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1321">URL 生成参考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1321">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1322">以下示例演示如何在给定路由值字典和 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection> 的情况下生成路由链接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1322">The following example shows how to generate a link to a route given a dictionary of route values and a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_Dictionary)]

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1323">上述示例末尾生成的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> 为 `/package/create/123`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1323">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generated at the end of the preceding sample is `/package/create/123`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1324">字典提供“跟踪包路由”模板 `package/{operation}/{id}` 的 `operation` 和 `id` 路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1324">The dictionary supplies the `operation` and `id` route values of the "Track Package Route" template, `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1325">有关详细信息，请参阅[使用路由中间件](#use-routing-middleware)部分或[示例应用](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples)中的示例代码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1325">For details, see the sample code in the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section or the [sample app](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1326"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> 构造函数的第二个参数是环境值的集合  。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1326">The second parameter to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> constructor is a collection of *ambient values*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1327">由于环境值限制了开发人员在请求上下文中必须指定的值数，因此环境值使用起来很方便。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1327">Ambient values are convenient to use because they limit the number of values a developer must specify within a request context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1328">当前请求的当前路由值被视为链接生成的环境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1328">The current route values of the current request are considered ambient values for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1329">在 ASP.NET Core MVC 应用 `HomeController` 的 `About` 操作中，无需指定控制器路由值即可链接到使用 `Home` 环境值的 `Index` 操作&mdash;。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1329">In an ASP.NET Core MVC app's `About` action of the `HomeController`, you don't need to specify the controller route value to link to the `Index` action&mdash;the ambient value of `Home` is used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1330">忽略与参数不匹配的环境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1330">Ambient values that don't match a parameter are ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1331">在显式提供的值会覆盖环境值的情况下，也会忽略环境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1331">Ambient values are also ignored when an explicitly provided value overrides the ambient value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1332">在 URL 中将从左到右进行匹配。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1332">Matching occurs from left to right in the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1333">显式提供但与路由片段不匹配的值将添加到查询字符串中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1333">Values explicitly provided but that don't match a segment of the route are added to the query string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1334">下表显示使用路由模板 `{controller}/{action}/{id?}` 时的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1334">The following table shows the result when using the route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1335">环境值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1335">Ambient Values</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1336">显式值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1336">Explicit Values</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1337">结果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1337">Result</span></span>                  |
| ---------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1338">控制器 =“Home”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1338">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1339">操作 =“About”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1339">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1340">控制器 =“Home”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1340">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1341">控制器 =“Order”，操作 =“About”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1341">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span></span> | `/Order/About`          |
| <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1342">控制器 = “Home”，颜色 = “Red”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1342">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1343">操作 =“About”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1343">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1344">控制器 =“Home”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1344">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1345">操作 =“About”，颜色 =“Red”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1345">action = "About", color = "Red"</span></span>        | `/Home/About?color=Red` |

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1346">如果路由具有不对应于参数的默认值，且该值以显式方式提供，则它必须与默认值相匹配：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1346">If a route has a default value that doesn't correspond to a parameter and that value is explicitly provided, it must match the default value:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute("blog_route", "blog/{*slug}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadPost" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1347">当提供 `controller` 和 `action` 的匹配值时，链接生成仅为此路由生成链接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1347">Link generation only generates a link for this route when the matching values for `controller` and `action` are provided.</span></span>

## <a name="complex-segments"></a><span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1348">复杂段</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1348">Complex segments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1349">复杂段（例如，`[Route("/x{token}y")]`）通过非贪婪的方式从右到左匹配文字进行处理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1349">Complex segments (for example `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) are processed by matching up literals from right to left in a non-greedy way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1350">请参阅[此代码](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293)以了解有关如何匹配复杂段的详细说明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1350">See [this code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) for a detailed explanation of how complex segments are matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ddfe7-1351">ASP.NET Core 无法使用[代码示例](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293)，但它提供了对复杂段的合理说明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddfe7-1351">The [code sample](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) is not used by ASP.NET Core, but it provides a good explanation of complex segments.</span></span>
